              <noteGrp>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">
                  <p>6.38.3 to 6.38.8 are in different metre (perhaps Indravajrā) with the same
                    content.</p>
                  <p>6.38.8 has only first hemistich.</p>
                  <p>Missing verses 6.38.30ab.</p>
                  <p>Metre break 6.38.13ab 6.38.17ab 6.38.21cd 6.38.28ab.</p>
                </note>

                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.39: <p>Missing verses 109ab, 110cd, 114cd,
                    115ab, 116cd, 117, 118, 119ab , 121cd, 122, 123ab, 125cd, 130, 131, 132, 133,
                    134ab, 135cd, 136, 137ab, 144ab, 147cd, 148ab, 137cd, 167, 171cd, 172, 173, 174,
                    190, 191, 193cd, 195, 196, 197, 198ab, 200cd, 201ab, 202ab, 204cd, 205, 206,
                    207, 211cd, 216ab, 219, 220, 221, 222, 223, 224, 225, 226, 227, 228, 229ab,
                    218cd, 232cd, 233, 234, 235, 236, 237, 238, 239, 240, 241, 242, 243, 244, 253cd,
                    254cd, 255, 256, 257, , 258, 264, 266ab, 267cd, 268ab, 277, 278, 279, 280ab,
                    281ab, 284cd, 286ab, 295-318, 319cd, 323</p>
                  <p>Additions 124a, 135a, 158a, 160, 201a-201c, 210a-210e, 232a-232b, 254a-254c,
                    273a-273g, 294a-294j, 320a-320b</p>
                  <p>- Chapter begins from verse no 104, folio no. 180r</p>
                  <p>- Verse 134ab is given after 128</p>
                  <p>- There are two folios named 183v. In the first 183v folio, there are 7 verses.
                    Content of these 7 verses (273a to 273g) seems different.</p>
                  <p>- Content of 294a to 294j, match with Cakradatta of Cakrapaṇḍita</p>
                </note>
                <note resp="Harshal Bhatt">Regarding 6.47L <p>Missing verses: 21ab, 22cd, 23ab,
                    29cd, 30ab, 54ab, 75cd, 76, 79ab</p>
                  <p>Additions: 4ef, 11, 12, 54.1ab, 73.1, 73.2, 73.3</p>
                  <p>Metre Break: 31ab, 80ab</p>

      <div n="6" type="sthāna">

        <div n="1" type="adhyāya">

          <!-- 157r:5 -->

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.1">athātaḥ aupadravikamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.3">saviśeṃ tu śatapūrva<cb/>madhyāyānāṃ tu kīrttite |
            <caesura/>
             vakṣye bahuvidhāṃ samyag uttare thānataḥ paraṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.4">idānīn ta<unclear extent="1" reason="torn" unit="syllable"
              >t</unclear><lb n="6"/> pravakṣyāmi tantram uttarasaṃjñitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             nikhilenopadṛṣyante yatra rogāḥ pṛtha<cb/>gvidhāḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.5">śālākyaśāstrāvihitā videhādhiyakīrttitā |
            <caesura/>
             ye ca vi<del>ra</del>staraśo dṛṣṭāḥ kumārābādha<cb/>hetavaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.6">ṣaṭsu kāyacikitsāsu ye coktāḥ paramarṣiṇā |
            <caesura/>
             upasargādayo ro<pb n="157v"/></l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.7"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.8">rogasādha<unclear>na</unclear>hetavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             asya tantrasya mahataḥ sāgarākāravarcasaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.9">ādāv evotta<cb/>māṃgasthāṃ rogā samabhidhāsyate |
            <caesura/>
             saṃkhyayā la<add place="above">kṣa</add>ṇaiś cāpi sādhyāsādhyakrameṇa ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.10">vidyādyaṃgulabāhulyaṃ svāṃguṣṭhodaramā<cb/>yataṃ |
            <caesura/>
             dvyaṅgulaṃ sarvataḥ sārdhaṃ bhiṣaṅ nayanabudbudaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.11">vṛttaṃ gostanakākāraṃ sarvabhū<lb n="2"/>taguṇodbhavaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             valaṃ mṛdbhyognito raktaṃ vātātkṛṣṇaṃ sitaṃ jalāt |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.12">ākāśādaśrumā<cb/>rgas tu jāyante netra budbude |
            <caesura/>
             dṛṣṭiś cātra yathā vakṣye tathā vidyādvicakṣaṇaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.13">netrāyāma<unclear>vi</unclear>bhāgas tu kṛṣṇammaṇḍalam ucya<cb/>te |
            <caesura/>
             kṛṣṇāt saptamam icchanti dṛṣṭiṃ dṛṣṭivido janāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.14">maṇḍalāni ca sandhīś ca paṭalā<lb n="3"/>ni ca locane |
            <caesura/>
             yathākramaṃ vijānīyāt pañcaṣaṭ ca ṣaḍ eva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.15">pakṣmavartmasita<cb/>śyāvadṛṣṭīnām maṇḍalāni tu |
            <caesura/>
             anupūrvantu catvāro madhyāduktā yathākramaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.16">pakṣmavarmagataḥ sandhi vartmaśuklaga<cb/>toparaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śuklakṛṣṇagatastvanyaḥ kṛṣṇadṛṣṭigatastathā |
            <caesura/>
             tataḥ kanīnikagataḥ<lb n="4"/> ṣaṣṭhaś cāpāṃgagaḥ smṛtaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.17">dve vartmapaṭale vidyāccatvāryanyāni cā<unclear>kṣṇi</unclear> tu |
            <caesura/>
             jāya<cb/>te timiraṃ yeṣu vyādhiparamadāruṇaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.18">tejo jalāśritaṃ bāhyaṃ teṣv anyapiśitāśritaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             medas tṛtīyam paṭalam ā<cb/>śritaṃ tv asthi cāparaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.19">pañcamāśaṃ samandṛṣṭes teṣāṃ bāhulyam iṣyate |
            <caesura/>
             sirāṇāṃ ka<lb n="5"/>ṇḍarāṇāñ ca medasaḥ kṛṣṇakasya ca </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.20">guṇā kṛṣṇātpa<unclear>raṃ</unclear> śleṣmā bandhanekṣṇoḥ
            sirā<cb/>yutaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             sirānusāribhir doṣair viguṇairūrdhvamāśritaiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.21">jāyante netrabhāgeṣu vyādhayaś cāstu dāruṇāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tatrā<cb/>vilaṃ sasaṃrambhamaśrukaṇḍūpadehavat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.22">gurūṣācoparāgādyair juṣṭañcāvyaktala<lb n="6"/>kṣaṇaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             saśūlaṃ vartmakośeṣu śukapūrṇṇābham eva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.23">vihanyamānaṃ rūpeṣu<cb/> kriyāsvakṣi yathāparaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             dṛṣṭvaivamdhīmāñjānīyāddoṣaiṇādhiṣṭhitantu tat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.24">tatra saṃ<unclear>ca</unclear>yamāsādya vidadhyāttatra<cb/> bheṣajaṃ
            |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.25">saṃkṣepataḥ kriyāyogo nidānaparivarjanaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             vātādīnāṃ pratīkāraḥ<pb n="158r"/>prokto vistarataḥ purā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.26">uṣṇābhitaptasya jalapraveśāddūrekṣaṇāt svapnaviparya<cb/>yācca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.27"><unclear>svesadrajo</unclear>dhūmaniṣevaṇādvā
            chardobhighātādvamanātiyogāt |
            <caesura/>
            <add>tathā dravānnātiniṣevaṇācca viṇmūtravāta<unclear>krama</unclear><cb/>nigrahācca
              |</add>
            <caesura/>
             prasaktasaṃrodanaśokakopācchirābhighātādatimadyayogāt |
            <caesura/>
            <unclear extent="4" reason="torn" unit="char"/><lb n="2"/>nāñca viparyayeṇa
            kleśābhighātādatimaithunācca |
            <caesura/>
             bāṣpagrahātsūkṣmanirīkṣaṇā<cb/>cca netre vikārāñjanayanti doṣāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.28">taistribhirdaśada<unclear><add extent="1" place="above" unit="char"
                >śa</add></unclear> ca kaphenāpyadhikāstrayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             raktajā ṣoḍaśa jñeyāḥ sarvajāḥ<cb/>pañcaviṃśati |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.29">bāhyau punardvau ca tathā rogāḥ ṣaṭsaptati smṛtāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             hatādhimantho nimi<lb n="3"/>śo dṛṣṭirgambhīrikā ca yā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.30">yac ca vātāhataṃ vartma te na sidhyanti vātajāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kā<cb/>coruṇau mārutajo yāpyo bhavati jānatā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.31">śuṣkākṣipākābhiṣyando yaś ca mārutaparyayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
            <unclear><add extent="1" place="inline" unit="pada">adhimanthānyavā<cb/>taś ca sādhyā
                mārutajeṣu te |</add></unclear>
            <caesura/>
             hrasvajāḍyajalasrāvāvasādhyau pittasambhavau |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.32">pari<lb n="4"/>mlāyī ca nīlī ca kāco yāpyaś ca tanmayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śuktisyandodhimanthaś ca tathāmlādhyu<cb/>ṣitañca yat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.33">dṛṣṭiḥ pittavidagdhā ca dhūmadarśī ca sidhyati |
            <caesura/>
            <unclear>su</unclear>srāvaḥ kaphaje sādhyo yāpyaḥ kācastu tanmayaḥ |<cb/></l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.34">abhiṣyandodhivātaś ca balāsagrathitantathā ||
            <caesura/>
             dṛṣṭiḥ śleṣmavidagdhā ca pothakyo laga<lb n="5"/>ṇaś ca yat |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.35">krimigranthipariklinnaṃ vartmaśuklārmapiṣṭakaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śleṣmopanā<cb/>hāḥ sādhyāste kathitā śleṣmajeṣu tu |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.36">raktasrāvojakājātaṃ śoṇitārśovraṇānvitaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             śukraṃ na sādhyaṃ kācantu yā<cb/>pyaṃ kṛṣṇaś ca tanmayaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.37">manthasyandau kliṣṭavartma harṣotpattau tathaiva ca |
            <caesura/>
             sirā<unclear>jātā</unclear>ñja<lb n="6"/>nākhyā ca sirājālaś ca yatsmṛtaṃ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.38">parvvaṇy athāvraṇaṃ śukraṃ lohitārma tathārju<cb/>naḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ete sādhyā vikāreṣu raktajeṣu bhavanti hi ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.39">pūyāsrāvo nākulāndhyamakṣīpākātyayojalī |
            <caesura/>
             rogā<cb/>asādhyāś catvāraḥ sarvajeṣu bhavanti hi |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.40">yāpyā vartmāvabandhastu pakṣmakopaḥ bha<lb n="7"
              />vi<unclear>plutaḥ</unclear> |
            <caesura/>
            <unclear>piṇḍā</unclear>kṣastu yo vyādhiḥ sirāsu piṭakā ca yā |
            <caesura/>
             prastāryarmā<cb/>dhīmāṃsārma snāyvarmotsaṅginī ca yā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.41">pūyālasaś cā<unclear extent="3" reason="torn" unit="syllables"
              >rbudaś ca </unclear> śyāvakardamavartmanī |
            <caesura/>
             tathārśovartmaśuṣkārśaḥ<cb/> śarkarāvartma eva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.42">aśophaśophai mahatau pākau bahalavartma ca |
            <caesura/>
             kumbhikinī<pb n="158v"/> vartmagatā bisavartma ca sidhyati |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.1.43">sanimitto nimittaś ca dvāvasādhyau ca bāhyataḥ |<cb/>
            <caesura/>
             rogāḥ ṣaṭsaptatistvete saṅgraheṇa prakīrttitāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.1"> athātaḥ sandhigatarogavijñānīyam <choice>
              <abbr type="suspension">vyā</abbr>
              <expan>vyā<ex>khyāsyāmaḥ</ex></expan>
            </choice> ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.2"/>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.3a"> navasandhyaśrajaś ca vartmajātāc e<lb n="2"/>kaviṃśati |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.4a">śuklabhāgaidasekaś ca catvāraḥ kṛṣṇabhāgajāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.5a"> sarvāśrayāḥ sapu<cb n="2"/>da<unclear>ma</unclear>
            dṛṣṭi<unclear/>dvādaśaivat tu |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.6a"> dvau tu sarvāśrayā vanyāvanimittanimittajau ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.3"> pūyālasaḥ soponāhaḥ srāvāḥ parva<cb n="2"/>ṇikālajī |
            <caesura/>
             krimigranthiś ca vijñeyā rogāḥ sandhigatā nava ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.4"> pakvaḥ śophaḥ sa <lb n="3"/>ndhijeyaḥ satodaḥ sravet pūyaṃ sa hi
            pūyālasākhyaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             granthir mahāndṛṣṭisandhāva<cb n="2"/>pākaḥ kaṇḍusrāvonīrūjāḥ sopanāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.5">gatvā sandhīnaśrumārgeṇa doṣāḥ śravantī vāsvāmimvikārāṃ kanīnāt |
            <caesura/>
            <cb n="3"/>tadviśrāvaṃ netranāḍīticaike tasyāliṅgaṃ kīrti yeṣye caturdhā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.6">pākāt sandhau saṃśra<lb n="4"/>vedyam sa pūyaṃ pūyāśrāvaḥ savikāro
            matas tu |
            <caesura/>
             śvetaṃ <unclear>skatraṃ</unclear> picchilaṃ yaḥ śrave<cb n="2"/>t tu śleṣmāśrāvaḥ
            savikāraḥ pradiṣṭaḥ |</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.7"> raktāśrāvaḥ śoṇitajovikāraḥ śravadūṣṇa tat tu raktam prabhūtaṃ |
            <caesura/>
            <cb n="3"/>hāridrābhaṃ pītam uṣṇaṃ jalam vā pittāśrāvaḥ saṃśravet sandhimadhyāt ||</l>


          <l xml:id="SS.6.2.8"> tāmrāṃ tanvīn dā<lb n="5"/>haśūlopapannāṃ vrūyād vaiḍyaḥ piṭakāṃ

          <l xml:id="SS.6.18.104"> ājena payasā piṣṭvā tāmrapātram pralepayet |
            <caesura/>
             saptakṛtvas tu tā varttyaḥ cchāyāśuṣkā <cb n="2"/>rujāpahā | </l>

            <caesura/>
             piṇḍāṃjanāni matimāṃ vidadhyāt tu yathāgadam iti ||</l>
